This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

This is previous problem file: 
(define (problem exploration-p1)
  (:domain exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen - location
    corridor - location
    laundry_room - location
    south_patio - location
    living_room - location
    bathroom - location
    bedroom - location
    south_bathroom - location
    north - direction
    south - direction
    east - direction
    west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at bedroom)
    (open kitchen west corridor)
    (open corridor east kitchen)
    (closed kitchen south south_patio)
    (open corridor north laundry_room)
    (open laundry_room south corridor)
    (closed corridor south south_patio)
    (closed corridor west living_room)
    (open laundry_room west bathroom)
    (open bathroom east laundry_room)
    (closed bathroom south south_bathroom)
    (open bathroom west bedroom)
    (open bedroom east bathroom)
  )
  (:goal
    (at south_patio)
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))

    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

  (:types location direction)

    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))

    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))

    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

 (define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)

    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))

(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)

Generated df and pf: 
 (define (domain exploration)
  (:types location direction)
  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (closed ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
    (open ?loc1 - location ?dir - direction ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2)) (open ?loc1 ?dir ?loc2))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (open ?from ?dir ?to))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
)
